Whilst every care is taken that the data inserted into the computer is accurate, the occasional error is inevitable.
Foreign players are dummies calculated from the top 30% of the ITTF World List. If a foreign player does not appear within this criteria
their dummy rating will be entered as zero apart from those players that regularly play in English tournaments.
You can update your nationality and county of affiliation by logging into the Table Tennis England members area.
Players in this booklet are eligible to play in England but are not necessarily eligible to represent England in International Competition.
Notes
If no nationality is specified on your Table Tennis England membership profile, your country will appear as "-" and you will be listed as a
Foreign Player.
If no county of affiliation is specified on your Table Tennis England membership profile, your county will appear as “-“.Under 13 Girls
